## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear dynamics / classical mechanics
**Analysis**: This is a nonlinear harmonic oscillator where acceleration depends on position, velocity, and possibly time. The nonlinearity can arise from anharmonic restoring forces (Duffing-type), nonlinear damping (van der Pol-type), or external time-dependent driving forces.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator (unforced): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (nonlinear damping)
- Driven harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (external periodic forcing)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (full Duffing with forcing)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order anharmonicity)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-modulated stiffness)
- Cubic damping oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity damping)
- General polynomial restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (asymmetric nonlinear potential)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (velocity-cubed damping)
- Mixed nonlinear: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**2 * v + c3 * v (combined Duffing + van der Pol)
- Driven van der Pol: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (1 + c2 * x**2) + c3 * sin(c4 * t) (driven self-excited oscillator)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x┬│, xŌüĄ) ŌåÆ symmetric potential well, preserving spatial symmetry of oscillation
- Even-power restoring forces (x┬▓) ŌåÆ asymmetric potential well, indicating broken spatial symmetry
- Velocity-position coupling terms like x┬▓*v ŌåÆ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-excited oscillations (van der Pol type)
- Cubic position term with opposite sign to linear term (c0*x - c1*x┬│) ŌåÆ double-well potential / softening spring behavior
- Cubic position term with same sign as linear term (-c0*x - c1*x┬│) ŌåÆ hardening spring with amplitude-dependent frequency
- Absence of explicit time dependence ŌåÆ autonomous system; presence of sin/cos(t) ŌåÆ externally driven system
- Product v*x^(even power) ŌåÆ energy-dependent dissipation that enables limit cycle behavior
- Odd powers of velocity (v, v┬│) in damping ŌåÆ dissipation symmetric under time reversal direction
